FACILITY   (SYNCH,2JPNJAE) ANNRI(BL04) beam line of MLF at J-PARC 2361300100013 
INC-SOURCE (SPALL) Spallation reaction in a mercury target        2361300100014 
           irradiated with 3-GeV protons (800 kW) .               2361300100015 
           The proton beams were supplied at a repetition rate of 2361300100016 
            25 Hz and in the "double-bunch mode", in which the    2361300100017 
           pulsed protons consist of two bunches, each with a     2361300100018 
           width of 100 ns, at intervals of 600 ns.               2361300100019 
           Produced neutrons were slowed down in a supercritical  2361300100020 
           para hydrogen moderator.                               2361300100021 
           Disk chopper with a semicircular shape was used to cut 2361300100022 
           the low-energy tail of neutron pulse.                  2361300100023

            -Size: 330 mm (diam.) and 203 mm in thickness         2361300100025

            -Crystal: 6Li(>95%) loaded glass (GS-20:Saint Gobain) 2361300100030

            -DAQ: CAEN V1720 (12bit, 250MHz)                      2361300100034 
           For background estimation, same size 7Li(>99.99%)      2361300100035 
           loaded glass detector (GS-30:Saint Gobain) was used.   2361300100036

ANALYSIS   Measurements with the carbon sample and                2361300200005 
           "Blank (no sample) " were used for background          2361300200006 
           estimation. The relative neutron spectrum was          2361300200007 
           estimated using the boron sample. The weighting        2361300200008 
           function was normalized by comparing the experimental  2361300200009 
           results of the Au sample with JENDL-5, 98.649 b.       2361300200010 
CORRECTION The dead-time correction was applied with the          2361300200011 
           extended dead-time model. Correction factors for       2361300200012 
           multiple scattering were deduced using the Monte-Carlo 2361300200013 
           simulation code PHITS. Self-shielding correction was   2361300200014 
           not applied. The influence was evaluated in the        2361300200015 
           resonance analysis in 23613.006.                       2361300200016
